 ham yah sabit kar denge ki hamaare muvakkilaritik kaa kangana ke sathkoi rishta nahin rahaa he

 ' unhone kaha, 'hamen notice bhejne vaale khel main koi dilchaspee nahin he

 jald hi tathy sabake saamne honge

 police uski talash kar rahi thi

 hariparvat thana par aalaa adhikari bhi pahunch gayi

 patni shanti se uski nahin banati thi

 use ek ladkaa or teen ladkiyaan hai

 pichley do maheene se bharat or pakistan ke bich parsparik sambadhon kii majboot kadi bani gita ke ghar-parivaar kaa pataa chalane ke baad saharsa ke ek gaanv kii rangath badal gai he

 ab jab bharat sarkaar ne gita kopakistan se waapas bharat laane kii kavayadshuru kar di he or use bihar ke saharsa kii beti ghoshit kar diya he, to gita ke ghar main jashn kaa maahaul he

 It is a matter of great pleasure that after a long time the lost baby girl of the village is coming back safely
 jharkhand main bhukh ke kaaran ek or mahila kii maut kii khabar he
 In Chatra district of here, 45-year-old Meena Mushar allegedly died of hunger
 bataaya ja rahaa he ki unhone pichley chaar dinon se kuch bhi nahin khaaya tha
 Let me tell you that in Giridih on Monday, a woman died due to hunger
 minaa musahar mul rup se bihar kii gaya kii rahane vaali thim, lekin kaaphi samay se chatra main hi rahati thim
 His son Gautam told that he and his mother had not eaten anything for the last 4 days
 jiske baad unki tabiyat bighad gai thi, lekin ilaaj or dawa ke paise nahin the
 Gautam told that when he loaded his mother on her shoulder and took her to the hospital, the doctors declared her dead
 giridih main bhi hui thi mautapako bataa den ki isse pehle somvaar ko jharkhand ke hi giridih jile ke madhuban thana kshetra ke magargadhi gaanv kii rahane vaali savitri devi kii maut ho gai thi

 unka kahana tha ki savitri devi ko teen dinon tak khaanaa nahin mila, jis vajah se maut ho gai

 savitri is sambandh main sabhi jaruri kagajaat do maheene pehle hi vibhaag ko saunp chuki thi
 65-year-old Savitri Devi has two sons who live out of work
 unki kamai itani nahin he ki ve ghar par paisa bhej saken
 Savitri Devi also did not get old age pension
 kendriya satarkta ayog (CVC) kii ore se kiye gaye ek haalia adhyayan main kaha gaya he ki sarkari karmchaaree ke khilaaf bhrashtachar ke kisi bade maamle ko nipataane main ausatan 8 saal kaa samay lag jaataa he
 This anti-corruption watchdog advises about 5000 vigilance cases every year
 first stage adwise (FSA) jaanch report par hota he, jabaki second stage adwise (SSA) antim nirnay se pehle kaa hota he
 The study said that it takes an average of eight years from the date of irregularity to give a final decision on a major case
 usne kaha ki FSA ke liye shuruaati jaanch karne or ise antim rup dene main ausatan kareeb do saal kaa samay lagata he
 According to the study, it is a matter of further concern that it takes more than two and a half years for the implementation of FSA, appointment of investigating officer, finalization of its report and sending departmental comments to SSA
 isi tarah anya charnon main bhi der hoti jaati he
 input language mangalvaar ko paak adhikrut kashmir main or pakistan ke andar bharat ne hawaii hamalaa kiya jisamen 300 se zyada aatanki maare gaye
 With this, Pakistan is deploying tanks and troops on the Indian border
 isse nipatane ke liye bharat bhi chaak-chauband he
 8 ships have been deployed to counter any attack on Porbandar port in Gujarat
 vahiin, paryatakon ke liye pakistan-bharat seemaa darshan band kar diya gaya he
 According to the information, Pakistan has started deployment of tank regiment across Kutch in Gujarat
 do dinon se yah kavayad chal rahi thi, jisamen mangalvaar ko teji dekhi gai
 The movement of the Pakistani army and the Rangers, just half a km away from the Vighakote border of Kutch, has increased
 seemaa paar sena ke jatthon kaa bhi movement dikh rahaa he
 Indian security agencies are monitoring these conditions
 bharat kii samudri seemaa khadau bandargah, paicrik or navalkhi sahit ilaakon main vishesh haclert he
 Soldiers are being deployed in the border villages
 saamaanya dinon main khaali rahane vaale watch tower par marine agency ke jawan tainaat kar die gaye hai
 There are 11 sensitive landing points in the area from Gosa to Miyani of Porbandar
 in jagahon par alert he
 Porbandar is 281 nautical miles from the port city of Karachi, Pakistan
 8 jahaaj porbandar pahunch gaye hai
 The Gujarat Maritime Board has ordered the Fisheries Guard to conduct a special investigation
 jaanch-kagajaat ke bina machuaaron ko samudr jane kii ijaajat kisi haal main nahin dene kaa nirdesh diya he
 The Seema Darshan has been closed to the people
 gujarat kii samudri seemaa kyon he sensitivegoratlab he ki 7 sitambar 1965 kii aadhi raat ke baad paanch pakistani vidhvansak bhartiya mandiron ke shahar dwarka se mahaj 5
 Came up to 8 nautical miles and started firing
 is ghatana se thik ek hafte pehle pakistani sena ne oparation grand slam ke naam se puri antarrashtriya seemaa par apana aakraamak sainya abhiyaan chalaaya tha
 India and Pakistan were then officially at war and the Pakistani Navy was in a fighting mood
 samudri tat ke samanaantar khadey dwitiya vishwa yuddh ke puraane bedon se saje pakistani yudhpot ne us raat gujarat ke tat par 50 gole daage the

 paak navy kii bambaari chaar minute tak jari rahi
 The Pakistani army had returned to Karachi fearing an air strike by the Indian Air Force based in Jamnagar
 lambe kad or majboot iraadon vaale endi mare ne somvaar ko khele gaye america open ke final mukaable main srbija ke novak jokovik ko haraakar 76 saal baad koi grand slam jeetne vaala britainvasi banane kaa gaurav hasil kiya
 Murray achieved this after losing four Grand Slam finals
 mare ne arthor aish stadium main vishwa ke duusare variyata praapt khilaadi jokovik ko 7-6 (12 / 10), 7-5, 2-6, 3-6, 6-2, se haraaya
 Murray had to wait for 28 Grand Slam events for his first Grand Slam title
 mare ne khitaab kii daud main is saal pehle daur main rus ke elex bogomolove ko 6-2, 6-4, 6-1 se haraaya
 He then defeated Ivan Dodig of Croatia 6–2, 6–1, 6–3 in the second round
 tisare daur main mare spain ke pheliciano lopage par haaavee rahe
 Murray won the match 7-6 (7 / 5), 7-6 (7 / 5), 4-6, 7-6 (7 / 4)
 lopage ko dhul chataane ke baad mare ne chauthe daur main canada ko milos raonic ko 6-2, 6-4, 6-2 se maat di

 / 10), 7-5, 2-6, 3-6, 6-2
 mare ne haal hi main samaapt landan olympics main apane desh ke liye ekal spardhaa kaa swarna jeeta tha
 In the title match, Murray defeated the world's highest seeded Roger Federer of Switzerland
 duusari ore, jokovik ke saamne america open khitaab bachaane vaala roger federer ke baad pehla khilaadi banane kii chunauti thi lekin vah isamen naakaam rahe
 Federer won the title five times consecutively between 2004 and 2008
 mare ne apni shandaar safalataa se scotland kaa naam roshan kiya or 1936 ke baad britain ke liye grand slam ekal khitaab jeetne vaale pehle khilaadi bane
 In 1936 Fred Perry won the US Open title
 mare kii yah jeet kaaphi myne rakhti he kyonki unhone lagaataar kai shikast khaane ke baad yah safalataa hasil kii he

 mare ko apane pehle grand slam khitaab ke liye 28 grand slam spardhaa kaa intjaar karnaa padaa

 iske baad unhone duusare daur main kroeshia ke evan dodig ko 6-2, 6-1, 6-3 se parajeet kiya
 Murray dominated Spain's Feliciano Lopez in the third round
 mare ne yah match 7-6 (7 / 5), 7-6 (7 / 5), 4-6, 7-6 (7 / 4) se apane naam kiya

 quarter final main mare kroeshia ke tejatarraar khilaadi marin silic ke khilaaf 3-6, 7-6 (7 / 4), 6-2, 6-0 se vijayi rahe or phir semifinal main check ganraajya ke thomas berdic ko 7-6 (12 / 10), 7-5, 2-6, 3-6, 6-2 se haraaya
 Murray won the singles gold for his country at the recently concluded London Olympics
 khitaabi mukaable main mare ne vishwa ke sarvocch variyata praapt khilaadi switzraland ke roger federer ko haraaya tha
